}</style> <script type="litespeed/javascript">var mpAjaxUrl='https://mokapota.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php';var currentCategory='',usedProducts=[],cards=[],favorites=[],startX=0,endX=0,allScreens={},selectedVariations={};document.addEventListener('DOMContentLiteSpeedLoaded',function(){allScreens={category:document.getElementById('mp-category-screen'),comparison:document.getElementById('mp-comparison-screen'),finished:document.getElementById('mp-finished-screen')};fetch(mpAjaxUrl+'?action=mp_get_categories').then(function(r){return r.json()}).then(function(cats){var wrap=document.getElementById('mp-categories');cats.forEach(function(cat){var btn=document.createElement('button');btn.textContent=cat.name;btn.onclick=function(){startCategory(cat.slug)};wrap.appendChild(btn)})});document.getElementById('mp-favorites-btn').onclick=toggleFavorites;document.getElementById('mp-compare-btn').onclick=showComparison;document.getElementById('mp-restart-btn').onclick=restart;document.getElementById('mp-restart-finished-btn').onclick=restart;document.getElementById('mp-compare-selected-btn').onclick=showComparison;document.addEventListener('keydown',function(e){if(e.key==='Escape'){closeModal();closeComparisonModal()}})});function showScreen(name){Object.values(allScreens).forEach(function(s){s.style.display='none'});allScreens[name].style.display='block'}
function startCategory(catSlug){currentCategory=catSlug;usedProducts=[];cards=[];showScreen('comparison');loadInitial()}
function restart(){currentCategory='';usedProducts=[];cards=[];favorites=[];selectedVariations={};document.getElementById('mp-products').innerHTML='';document.getElementById('mp-favorites-list').innerHTML='';document.getElementById('mp-favorites-list').style.display='none';updateFavorites();updateCompareButton();showScreen('category')}
function loadInitial(){Promise.all([loadOne(),loadOne()]).then(function(prods){cards=prods.filter(function(p){return p});render()})}
function loadOne(){return fetch(mpAjaxUrl,{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'},body:new URLSearchParams({action:'mp_get_one_product',category:currentCategory,used:JSON.stringify(usedProducts)})}).then(function(r){return r.json()}).then(function(p){if(!p||p.end)return null;usedProducts.push(p.id);return p})}
function render(){var box=document.getElementById('mp-products');box.innerHTML='';if(cards.length===0)return;cards.forEach(function(p,i){var c=cardHTML(p,i);c.style.opacity=0;box.appendChild(c);setTimeout(function(){c.style.opacity=1},50);addSwipe(c,i)});updateFavoritesList()}
function cardHTML(p,index){var d=document.createElement('div');d.className='mp-card';d.innerHTML='<img src="'+(p.image||'')+'" alt="'+p.title+'"><div class="mp-card-content"><h3>'+p.title+'</h3><div class="mp-excerpt">'+p.excerpt+'</div><div class="mp-actions"><button onclick="selectProduct('+index+')">Bunu Seç</button><button onclick="addFavorite('+index+')">Kenara Ayır</button></div></div>';return d}
function selectProduct(selectedIndex){var keep=cards[selectedIndex];var removeIndex=selectedIndex===0?1:0;var oldCard=document.getElementById('mp-products').children[removeIndex];if(oldCard){oldCard.style.transform='translateX('+(removeIndex===0?-100:100)+'%) scale(0.9)';oldCard.style.opacity=0}
cards=[keep];loadOne().then(function(p){if(!p){showFinished();return}
cards.push(p);setTimeout(function(){render()},200)})}
function addFavorite(index){var p=cards[index];if(!p||!p.id)return;if(favorites.find(function(f){return f.id===p.id}))return;if(favorites.length>=3){showModal(p);return}
var productsEl=document.getElementById('mp-products');if(!productsEl||!productsEl.children[index]){favorites.push(p);updateFavorites();updateFavoritesList();updateCompareButton();return}
var cardEl=productsEl.children[index];var cardRect=cardEl.getBoundingClientRect();var favBtn=document.getElementById('mp-favorites-btn');var favRect=favBtn.getBoundingClientRect();var clone=cardEl.cloneNode(!0);clone.style.position='fixed';clone.style.left=cardRect.left+'px';clone.style.top=cardRect.top+'px';clone.style.width=cardRect.width+'px';clone.style.height=cardRect.height+'px';clone.style.zIndex='10000';clone.style.transition='all 0.8s ease-out';clone.style.pointerEvents='none';document.body.appendChild(clone);setTimeout(function(){clone.style.left=favRect.left+'px';clone.style.top=favRect.top+'px';clone.style.transform='scale(0.1)';clone.style.opacity='0'},50);setTimeout(function(){clone.remove();favorites.push(p);updateFavorites();updateFavoritesList();updateCompareButton();favBtn.classList.add('pulse');setTimeout(function(){favBtn.classList.remove('pulse')},400);cardEl.style.transform='scale(0)';cardEl.style.opacity='0';setTimeout(function(){var keepIndex=index===0?1:0;var keep=cards[keepIndex];cards=[keep];loadOne().then(function(newP){if(!newP){showFinished();return}
cards.push(newP);setTimeout(function(){render()},200)})},300)},850)}
function showModal(newProduct){var modal=document.getElementById('mp-modal');var favWrapper=modal.querySelector('.mp-modal-fav');favWrapper.innerHTML='';favorites.forEach(function(f,i){var d=document.createElement('div');d.className='mp-fav-card';d.innerHTML='<img src="'+f.image+'" alt="'+f.title+'"><h4>'+f.title+'</h4>';d.onclick=function(){favorites.splice(i,1);favorites.push(newProduct);updateFavorites();updateFavoritesList();updateCompareButton();closeModal()};favWrapper.appendChild(d)});modal.style.display='flex'}
function closeModal(){document.getElementById('mp-modal').style.display='none'}
function updateFavorites(){var btn=document.getElementById('mp-favorites-btn');btn.textContent='Kenara Ayırdıklarım ('+favorites.length+' Ürün)'}
function updateCompareButton(){var compareBtn=document.getElementById('mp-compare-btn');var compareFinishedBtn=document.getElementById('mp-compare-selected-btn');if(favorites.length>=2){compareBtn.style.display='block';if(compareFinishedBtn)compareFinishedBtn.style.display='block'}else{compareBtn.style.display='none';if(compareFinishedBtn)compareFinishedBtn.style.display='none'}}
function updateFavoritesList(){var list=document.getElementById('mp-favorites-list');list.innerHTML='';favorites.forEach(function(p){var d=document.createElement('div');d.className='mp-fav-card';d.innerHTML='<a href="'+p.url+'" target="_blank"><img src="'+p.image+'" alt="'+p.title+'"><h4>'+p.title+'</h4></a>';list.appendChild(d)})}

function updateVariation(productId){var card=document.querySelector('[data-product-id="'+productId+'"]');var selects=card.querySelectorAll('.mp-variation-select');var btn=card.querySelector('button');if(!selectedVariations[productId])selectedVariations[productId]={};var allSelected=!0;var selectedAttrs={};selects.forEach(function(sel){var attrKey=sel.dataset.attribute;var attrValue=sel.value;if(attrValue){selectedAttrs[attrKey]=attrValue;selectedVariations[productId][attrKey]=attrValue}else{allSelected=!1}});if(allSelected){var variations=JSON.parse(card.dataset.variations||'[]');var matchedVariation=null;for(var i=0;i<variations.length;i++){var variation=variations[i];var matches=!0;for(var attr in selectedAttrs){var selectedVal=selectedAttrs[attr].toLowerCase().trim();var varVal=variation.attributes[attr];if(!varVal||varVal===''){continue}
